< review>
As soon as you walk in you are standing in line, as cashier is straight ahead. They only have tacos and mulitas and drinks. We ordered Asada and Adobada (al-pastor) tacos. The size is smaller than regular tortilla but slightly larger than a small street taco tortilla. The asada taco comes with onions, cilantro, avacado, and salsa( red, spicy but not much). To us the tacos were good with a good charcoal flavor. The Adobada tacos lacked juiciness and the sauce for that wasn't as flavorful as other places. Tortillas are handmade for Asada (1tortilla) tacos not sure Adobada (2 tortilla).</review>

This review is well overdue. I have been with The Movement Warehouse for 2+ years because a coworker asked me to go and I have been hooked ever since. I was always hesitant about group workout classes due to previous sports injuries and I needed to ensure someone focused on my form. Mike, Meagan, and Dani are amazing and always help when needed. They know my injuries and will create a modification for me when necessary. The great thing about the modification is that it's not any easier. It's still an exercise that pushes me without the pain and I don't feel any less accomplished.

Mike has cultivated a fitness community that goes well beyond just diet and exercise. The Movement Warehouse is a family of people that all want to better themselves in one way or another. We also have a TON of FUN while doing it. Not only do we enjoy our workouts together, but there are events outside of the classes that happen. There are social events, yoga classes, game nights, and other wellness gatherings that help you connect with people.

The Movement Warehouse community is filled with people from various workout, athletic, and health and fitness backgrounds and levels. The one constant is we all love to come here and we all appreciate the work they put in to help us improve. I am faster, stronger, and more flexible since joining and I am truly appreciative of everything they have done since I joined.

Mike, Meagan, and Dani are amazing and I know they can't wait to help you meet and surpass your goals.<//text>

< Text>
Found the Movement Warehouse about 9 months ago through a couple friends and was talked into giving it a try.  At the time, I was a bit hesitant to go lift weights and jump around the gym in what I assumed to be a "cross fit" atmosphere since I was coming off a recent back surgery.  Boy was I wrong.

The team of trainers (led by head trainer Mike) are amazing to work with.  Have an old injury that's holding you back?  There's a way to train and eliminate risk of re-injury with this team.  They always have your best interest in mind and can recommend alternative exercises if something makes you uncomfortable or is a health risk for you.  The folks that workout here are an amazing group and are super welcoming, really incredible people.

After 9 months, the results are amazing!  My core strength is stronger than ever which has accelerated the results of my back surgery, my upper body has actual defined muscles which I haven't seen in 10 years, and the lower/leg workouts have increased my mobility and racing speed.

Bottom line, if you are looking for results, look no further than The Movement Warehouse.  If you are willing to put in the time and trust with this team, you will get stronger, faster, and live a healthier lifestyle as a result.

Final thought for those with a difficult schedule, The Movement Warehouse has amazing hours ranging from 530a-630p and weekend classes which makes it incredibly easy to get into the gym 4-6x per week.

< text>
One expects the crunch of nuts in a "Double Almond Chocolate   Machiatto (sp?)"ice cream sundae. Upon experiencing the lack of even a single almond sliver in the dish one understands disappointment and chagrin; the concoction gets its name from almond milk. Hence, the machiatto in the name should have been the tell tale hint! I drink my coffee black so I associate machiatto with coffee (cafe machiatto) - the lack of any discernible flavor of coffee also left a sense of unfulfilled want. The one star in this review is for the friendly but apologetic attendant. For those allergic to nuts - of any kind -in the ice cream this place will certainly not let you down. For those who enjoy the crunchiness of nuts, have them add the nuts or seek le paradis in another parlor.</text>

The curriculum involves a lot of studying and memorization in addition to developing the necessary driving skills.

Although I've been a licensed Class C driver for 13 years, I needed to learn the differences with Class A driving which aren't so obvious. I was glad to move through the process quickly, dedicating a portion of my week to studying and practice. Sharif and Lucky helped me perfect the essential parking maneuvers, and J.B. was instrumental in getting me comfortable with driving on city streets and on the highway. I was nervous during my test, but I felt well prepared with a solid foundation in knowledge and practice. I was glad to be studying during the recent DMV closure, and the school was very proactive in securing my test date and ensuring that I was well prepared and confident despite my nerves.

This is a busy school, and the price is unbeatable. I've enjoyed learning with and from fellow students, as I feel that the best way to prove one's knowledge of a subject is to be able to teach it. We learn by doing, and I was pleasantly surprised to be thrown into practical learning on my first day of attendance. < Text>
National Truck Driving School

I did my research on several different truck driving schools in the Bay Area. I was looking for the cheapest because my budget was low. Most schools were way beyond my budget. The schools I research wanted like up to $5,000 and more.

I contacted National Truck Driving School in Hayward California and ask them their price. When they told me I almost fell on the floor. It was within my budget and they do payment plans. I made sure I check the Bureau to see if they are legit and they are and have no discipline complains. The school is in full compliance with the law.

I went in to go over their student catalog and was amazed that all student get four months to finish the program. Other truck driving school programs out there only gives you six to eight weeks to complete.
I started my Class A training the next day and worked on it for two weeks. I boss told me I did not need a Class A and just do a Class B because we need you working now. I went back to the school and told them my situation with my job and I had no problems with them on down grading from A to B, everything was smooth.

Here I am 2 months later I just past my Class B with air brakes, thanks to their fantastic instructors, ShareeF and Lucky. They both work with Class B and Class A students but Lucky, is more focus on Class B. They both took their time to teach me how to drive and past the DMV test. This school cost is well worth it. If your funds our low and you need to get your Class A or B, this is the place.<//Text>

Let me tell you, this school wouldn't be getting a 4 from me if it wasn't for the instructors and the support I received.  Lucky is the best instructor for the Class B!  Learning from him was easy. He was always supportive and he is very knowledgeable in both class A & B!  Sharif was also very easy to learn from. They both know their stuff and they are always up to date with how DMV tests. Abdul is the Office Manager, he was able to answer my questions and get me started at the school. He was accommodating with my work schedule and when it came down to getting an appointment for me he was able to move things around!  He even helped me understand the air brakes. All of them are great people.  The only negative to this school is that the bus and trucks are very old and needs to be fixed all the time.  So students would have to wait or reschedule test appointments because of the vehicles. (I was one of those students) I give the instructors so much praise because they are still able to get their students licensed after 1 or 2 tries!  I hope you guys get a new bus soon!  Again...thanks Lucky for all that you did for me!   It took just one try for me!  If your planning on going to this school...make sure you learn from Lucky and Sharif!  They are the best!<//review>
